 rajasthan ke ballebaajon ne beshak saraahneey pradarshan kiya lekin match kaa shreshth khilaadi kaa puraskaar gendbaaj james folownar ko mila

 unhen parvinder awana ne mandeep singh ke haathon kaich karaayaa

 dravid ne 12 gendon par do chauke lagaae
 Dravid's wicket fell on the first ball of the eighth over
 isi over kii paanchavin gend par praveen ne stuart binni (0) ko wicket ke peeche kaich karakar rajasthan royles ko teesraa jhatka diya

 Party leaders have not understood why Sushma Swaraj has publicly stated herself instead of putting her words on the party's highest decision making body, the Parliamentary Board
 yah kaha ja rahaa he ki vinod sharma ko lekar party ke virodh ko haryana janhit congress ke netaa kuldeep vishnoi ko bataa diya gaya tha, jiske baad unhone brihaspativaar ko dilli main vinod sharma ke saath hone vaali saajha press conference ko radd kar diya tha
 After that, why did Sushma need to make her protest about Vinod Sharma public? darasal, bijepi main sab kuch saamaanya nahin he
 After the announcement of Narendra Modi as the Prime Ministerial candidate in September last year, the leadership issue was now resolved
 tab is faisle ko lekar bijepi ke sheershasth netaa laalkrishna adwani ne rajnath singh ko likhe apane patr ko saarvajanik kar naaraazgi jaahir kar di thi, lekin dhire-dhire unke tewaron main bhi narmi aati dikhaai di
 Recently, at the party's national council meeting at Delhi's Ramlila Maidan, he had hoped that Modi would prove to be a better prime minister
 tab yah mana gaya ki modi kii ummidavaari ko lekar unki naaraazgi dur ho gai he or khud pradhanmantri banane kii unki mahatvakanksha par vaastaviktaa ko dekhakar viraam lag gaya he
 But it is not so
 chahen adwani hon, murali manohar joshi hon yaa phir sushamaa swaraj
 With the announcement of the dates of Lok Sabha elections, the resentment of these leaders is coming out differently
 jahaan adwani khud apane munh se hi gandhinagar se loksabhaa chunaav ladane kii ichha jataa chuke hai, vahiin murali manohar joshi ke samarthakon ne narendra modi ke banaras se chunaav ladane kii khabaron ke bich unke poster vahaan lagavane shuru kar die hai
 And now through Twitter, Sushma Swaraj has made her protest public
 vishleshkon kaa maananaa he ki sushamaa kii koshish daagi netaaon se khud ko dur dikhaakar apni chhavi ko durust rakhane kii he
 Significantly, Sriramulu is close to the Reddy brothers of Bellary
 kisi vakt ye reddy bandhu sushamaa swaraj ke kareebi maane jate the, lekin janardan reddy par avaidh khanan ke aarope lagane or sibiai dwaara unki giraftaar ke baad se sushamaa ne inase duuri bananaa shuru kar diya
 It is believed that the merger of Sriramulu into the BJP will mean the return of the Reddy brothers to the BJP
 sushamaa swaraj ko lagata he ki agar aisa hoga to party main unke virdohi ye aarope laga sakate hai ki unheen kii vajah se reddy badhuon kii party main vaapasi hui he
 That is why, by making public opposition to Sriramulu, he has kept it on record that he is against the tainted Reddy brothers
 yahi kissa vinod sharma kaa bhi he, jinke bete manu sharma ko model jesica laal kii hatya main umrakaid kii sajaa hui he
 Vinod Sharma is the powerful Brahmin leader of Haryana and played a big role in turning Hooda's minority government into a majority
 vinod sharma ke kareebi haryana main prachaar kar rahe the ki sushamaa kii vajah se vinod sharma bijepi yaa uski sahyogi party se judane ja rahe hai or iskaa pardaafash karne ke liye hi sushamaa ko apana virodh saarvajanik karnaa padaa
 One faction in the BJP still hopes that if the party does not do well under Modi's leadership in the Lok Sabha elections, the path of someone else to become Prime Minister instead of Modi may be cleared
 isi ummid ke chalate laalkrishna adwani aresas ke na chaahane ke baavjood loksabhaa chunaav ladane ke liye na sirf icchhuk hai, balki apni ichha saarvajanik kar party par dabaav bhi bana rahe hai
 Interestingly, even before NDA was declared as the Prime Ministerial candidate for the 2009 Lok Sabha elections, Advani used to say that according to the tradition of the British Parliament, the Leader of the Opposition in the Lok Sabha is the PM in waiting
 lekin disambar, 2009 main sushamaa swaraj ke loksabhaa main vipaksh kaa netaa banane ke baad se pichley paanch saal main adwani ne ek baar bhi yah baat nahin kahi he or na hi saarvajanik rup se khud ko pradhanmantri pad kii daud se baahar kiya he
 After the break-up of the BJP and JDU alliance that lasted for 17 years, there is also news of a split in the Bihar BJP
 bijepi vidhayak dal kii baithak main aadha darjan vidhayak shaamil nahin hue
 Significantly, on Wednesday, Chief Minister Nitish Kumar will prove his majority in the Bihar Assembly
 is bich khabar yah bhi he ki congress vidhayak nitish ko samarthan de sakate hai
 Actually, Chief Minister Nitish Kumar has to prove his majority in the assembly and before that BJP had called a legislature party meeting, but it did not have 6 mlas of the party Prem Kumar, Rana Gangeshwar, Amarnath Gami, Veena Singh, Avinash Kumar and Vikram Kunwar
 nitish ko bahumat sabit karne ke liye 4 or vidhayakon kaa samarthan chahie or bijepi ke aadha darjan vidhayakon ke baithak main naa jane se atakalon kaa bazaar garm he
 Meanwhile, BJP mlas elected Nand Kishore Yadav as the leader of the legislative party in this meeting and he will be the leader of the opposition in the assembly
 bijepi kaa kahana he ki janata ne endie ko apana vot diya tha or gathbandhan tuutane se janata ke faisle kaa apmaan hua he
 BJP said that it will oppose the process of getting Nitish Kumar's confidence vote again
 dost se dushman banane ke baad jediu or bijepi vidhayakon kaa buudhvaar ko pehali baar vidhansabha main aamanaa-saamana hoga
 After breaking ties with the BJP, the Nitish government has called a special session of the Legislative Assembly to prove its majority in the House
 aankadon par gaur karen to nitish ke liye vishwaas mat hasil karnaa kaaphi aasaan he
 In the Bihar assembly with 234 seats, the JDU needs the support of 122 mlas for a majority
 jediu ke paas 118 vidhayak hai or use 4 nirdaleey vidhayakon ne bhi samarthan dene kaa elaan kiya he
 At the same time, after BJP mlas absent from the meeting, now the way for Nitish is looking more easy
 argedy mukhiya lalu yadav ne vishwaas mat ke dauraan nitish ke khilaaf vot dene kaa elaan to kiya he, lekin unhen bhi maaloom he ki number nitish ke saath he
 It is also easy to get Nitish's trust vote because four Congress mlas have decided not to participate in voting
 itnaa hi nahin sipiai ke 1 vidhayak ne nitish ko samarthan dene kii baat kahi he
 Independent mlas 'vinay Bihari, Pawan Kumar Jaiswal, Dulal Chand Goswami and Somprakash Singh' rode in a car to attend the JDU meeting and reached the Chief Minister's residence on one of the roads
